Foreign Important Telegrams

Director of International Labour Bureau, Thomas, Passed Away Yesterday 85

Havas Paris, 8th The former French cabinet minister and current Director of the International Labour Bureau, Thomas, was still talking with friends in a coffee shop near the Saint-Lazare station in Paris at midnight yesterday when he suddenly felt unwell, turned pale, and collapsed. He was taken to the Poing Hospital for examination, where he passed away after a short time. The Poing Hospital is also where President Doumer died.

Havas Paris, 7th Mr. Thomas, Director of the International Labour Bureau, graduated from the French École Normale Supérieure and was elected as a member of parliament several times, belonging to the Socialist Party. During the Great War, he served as Minister of Armaments. After the establishment of the International Labour Organization in Geneva, Thomas took charge of it. He was a skilled orator, excelled in administration, and worked tirelessly. He was a key figure in the Geneva International Organization and was particularly concerned about labour organizations. He travelled to the Far East several years ago to investigate labour conditions.

French Old National Assembly to Convene Today to Elect Successor President 86

President of the Senate Lebrun is Promising

Second Vote Still in Progress

Unaffected by Assassination

National News Agency Paris, 7th For the position of successor President, Senate President Lebrun is the most promising. When the National Assembly meets at the Palace of Versailles on Tuesday to hold the election of the new President, Lebrun will serve as chairman. When the late President Doumer was elected as the national leader by the President of the Senate last May 13th, Lebrun succeeded to the position of Senate President. Lebrun was also a candidate for President last year, and is now supported by several factions of the Right, so his election is highly likely. Lebrun is 61 years old, has a distinguished political record, and has served as a cabinet member several times. Although he belongs to the Right, he is known for his stability. His profession, like that of the current President of the United States, is that of a mining engineer. When the National Assembly meets, members of the House of Representatives will still attend as old members, because although the new members will be elected tomorrow, they cannot be convened before the end of this week.

National News Agency Paris, 7th Today, due to respect for the late President Doumer, all political parties have announced a truce. Therefore, the scheduled campaign meetings for the evening have been suspended. Before the new President is elected, the position of head of state will be temporarily held by Prime Minister Tardiou, according to precedent.

Reuters Paris, 8th The second round of voting in the general election began at 8:00 a.m. this morning to elect 359 members of the House of Representatives. Although it is not as exciting as in the past, the number of voters is still large. The assassination will not have a significant impact on the general election. However, the public's demand for strict surveillance of foreigners entering France may cause the extreme left to lose many votes, as the public views the Communist Party as violent. Senate President Lebrun has agreed to be a candidate for President. Whether former Prime Minister Painlevé will be the candidate for President from the Left is still in doubt.

Goguloff Accused of Murder 87

Of Firm Disposition and Sound Mind

Hates Communist Ideology and is Eccentric

Assassination of French President Doumer 88

Said to be in Revenge for Personal Grievances

Little Political Motivation

-Statement of Goguloff's Wife-

Comintern Issues Statement

Opposes Individual Acts of Terror

Reuters Paris, 7th Goguloff was formally charged with murder this afternoon. The authorities will appoint a lawyer to defend him on Sunday. The Russian Ambassador to France visited the hospital yesterday to inquire about his condition and looked sorrowful upon leaving. He later sent a counselor to Prime Minister Tardiou to express condolences. The Russian counselor described the crime as an act of arrogance and baseness.

Havas Paris, 7th Regarding the character of the assassin Goguloff and the nature of the assassination, it is feared that accurate information may not be obtained in the near future. A supplementary report from the capital of Czechoslovakia proves that Goguloff had a very bad reputation among the Russian expatriates there. He was generally regarded as a political activist. Goguloff studied medicine in Rostov, Russia, in 1922, and completed his studies in the capital of Czechoslovakia in 1926. In 1927, he went to the Soviet Union and worked in the sanitation bureau of a certain area in the Kustanai province, using the alias "Chulkov" and belonging to the Communist Party. Later, he returned to Czechoslovakia and lived in the suburbs of the capital. He showed his Communist Party membership card to the local officials there. He once planned to go to France, but he did not because he started organizing the so-called "Pan-Russian Peasants' Party" in Czechoslovakia. The party he organized was actually just a new Bolshevik party.

National News Agency Paris, 7th The wife of Goguloff, the assassin of French President Doumer, was brought here from Monaco today. After six hours of continuous investigation at the police station, it was concluded that Goguloff's motive for the assassination was revenge for personal grievances, and that political motives were minor. After a long interrogation, Goguloff's wife denied that her husband had any signs of mental illness, but she said that he often expressed hatred for the French government because he had been expelled from France twice, and therefore harbored resentment. Coupled with his lack of intelligence, he was involved in politics, which was the motive for the murder. Goguloff's wife is Swiss. It is said that although Goguloff hated the Communist Party deeply, he was not a restorationist. He was stubborn and regarded national revival as his mission. He also made a great vow to save the world from communist trampling. The reason why his thinking was so stubborn was that he had been wounded in the head by shrapnel during the European War. Goguloff was still studying at a medical school in Moscow at the beginning of the European War. He immediately enlisted in the army and was discharged as disabled in 1917. He lived in Lapinskaga in the Caucasus Mountains. His father owned land, but after his father's death, the property was confiscated by the Soviet authorities, which made Goguloff hate the Communist Party even more. In 1921, his mother died, and Goguloff fled from Russia to Kurage and resumed his medical studies. He graduated from medical school and interned in a hospital. Later, he practiced medicine in Mahren via, and the situation was very good. The city belonged to Czechoslovakia, but Goguloff was forbidden to practice medicine because he did not join Czech nationality. Goguloff then went to France to practice medicine in Paris, but suffered various setbacks. Then he and his wife entered Monaco and settled down. Goguloff's life has been like this. He is rich in emotions and complex in thought, and he also prides himself on literature, writing two novels and a collection of poems, but readers say that they are very superficial.

Reuters Prague, 7th The Dean of the Obstetrics and Gynecology College here, Yeli, declared today that Goguloff obtained his medical degree through deception. Goguloff claimed that his father was a former officer of the Russian Imperial Guard and his mother was a nun. Goguloff often felt depressed in spring and summer and was examined by a neurologist. It is said that Goguloff often practiced shooting targets in his garden all night long.

TASS Moscow, 7th The Moscow newspapers today published a detailed biography of Goguloff, the assassin of French President Doumer, proving that he was an absolute hater of Bolshevism and opposed to the Soviet system. The newspapers also excerpted the constitution of the so-called "Green Party" (Pan-Russian Peasants' Party), which was signed by Goguloff as the leader and circulated abroad, indicating that the assassin was indeed a counter-revolutionary activist. It is said that some deliberately pointed out that Goguloff was a near-Bolshevik and engaged in agitation for the Third International, apparently to cover up his terrorist acts and use the assassination of this political figure to provoke disputes between the Soviet Union and other countries. The "Green Party Constitution" contains a declaration by Goguloff and others to Russian readers, denouncing the Soviet authorities as "Jewish assassins and bandits in the Soviet Union," saying that the only way out at present is to create a coup, a new revolution, kill all Soviet leaders, communists, assassins, robbers, enemies of workers and peasants, and hang all members of the Cheka (page 12 of the constitution). It also said that if the Soviet Union goes to war with Poland, Romania, China, etc., you should surrender to the enemy and become prisoners, because the enemy can clothe, feed, and protect you, which is a thousand times better than your communist and Cheka friends treat you. Without waiting for the war, quickly escape the country privately, kill your officers, carry your weapons, and say goodbye to Stalin forever (page 5). It also said, return all power to the non-party areas of Russia, and overthrow the Communist Party (page 12). After quoting the above paragraphs, the Moscow newspapers stated that the claim made by some that Goguloff's peasant party had a relationship with the Third International was a great farce. The newspaper then pointed out that after the assassin of the German embassy counselor, Stern, was executed, the White Russian Federation held a memorial meeting in Paris, and the speakers all praised the terrorist means of harming foreign political figures, calling it the only good way to fight against the Soviet Union. Also, the texts published by Kerensky in the Teni newspaper, issues 151 and 153, also praised Stern's terrorist acts in the same way.

Havas Paris, 7th The assassin of the French President was imprisoned at 9:00 p.m. last night and brought to court at 3:00 p.m. today. He was informed that the President had died and that his assassination of the President had changed from attempted murder to completed murder. Goguloff's wife was found in Monaco and voluntarily came to Paris to explain everything, but she said that she knew nothing about her husband's assassination plan. Goguloff had previously joined a certain faction and was slightly involved in an anarchist group, which attacked both the White and Red parties in the South Russia during the Russian civil war. After Goguloff fled Russia in 1921, he lived in Prague, Czechoslovakia, for a long time, studying medicine. His father was an officer of the former Russian Imperial Guard and later suffered from wind disease, and died paralyzed. His mother was a French nun. Goguloff had entered the Petersburg Army Primary School and often associated with nobles. The Russian Empress gave him a small diamond. During the European War, he was injured in the head in the Bukovina campaign. After the Russian Revolution, he first became a mason, then studied medicine at the University of Prague, Czechoslovakia. Because he did not obtain a degree, he could not practice medicine, so he went to Berlin to live, wanting to make a living by writing. He had written several books, including a small collection of poems. Goguloff said that in his works, he created a new literature of naturalism. He then planned to organize a "Pan-Russian Peasants' Party" and printed a plan, with only Goguloff as the member. His plan said that the way to save the world is only through war to demand Russia from the Russians, and promoting peace will be the end of Europe. Goguloff also said that he had invented special machinery that could defeat many enemies without suffering losses. Russian people in Prague said that Goguloff had intended to organize a green army to attack the Soviets from the Far East. Some factional newspapers seem not to believe the assassin's declaration. The monarchist newspaper of the Russian expatriates in Paris clearly acknowledged that Goguloff was a provocateur. The newspaper said that when Kutepov was kidnapped in Paris, a certain group was very much noticed by people at the time, and Goguloff had some relationship with this group. The royalist newspaper even said that Goguloff's assassination was related to the actions of the Koreans in Shanghai. The radical socialist newspaper strongly opposed the interpretation of the assassin's actions by the extreme right-wing newspapers and explained to the people that the assassin was only acting as a madman and had no meaning at all, while the extreme right-wing newspapers pointed out that it had political color. This statement contains a role and should not be taken lightly. The French Communist Party's newspaper also pointed out that the assassin was a provocateur, saying that Goguloff's actions were an anti-Soviet provocation.

TASS Moscow, 7th The newspapers here published a statement by the Comintern on the assassination of French President Doumer. The statement was signed by representatives of the Communist Parties of Germany, England, Russia, Czechoslovakia, France, Italy, and Japan. According to the Havas report, French Prime Minister Tardiou and his cabinet members held a meeting and issued an official document stating that the assassin of Doumer belonged to a "Pan-Russian Party with a near-Bolshevik nature" and was instructed by the Third International. The Executive Committee of the Comintern is deeply indignant at this rogue fabrication, believing that the intention of the fabricator is obviously to cover up the terrorist acts of the White Russians and blame the Comintern. The statement also said that Goguloff is a deadly enemy of communism, as evidenced by his writings and his confession, and the whole world knows that the Comintern is a group of international working classes that most resolutely oppose individual acts of terrorism.

The World Mourns the Death of Doumer 89

Geneva Disarmament Conference Suspended

British Court to Wear Mourning for a Week

Havas Paris, 7th President Doumer's remains are displayed in the Green Hall of the Presidential Palace. His family will go to guard the coffin from this afternoon. With a few exceptions, everyone can go to pay respects. The late president is wearing a formal dress, with a first-class medal of honor on the chest. The wound on the jaw is almost invisible because the wound has stopped bleeding and is covered with a small bandage, which is enough to conceal it. Crowds gathered outside the residence, and the police lined up to block them, so the order was not disturbed. Prime Minister Tardiou arrived at the Presidential Palace at 3:25 p.m. Madame Doumer immediately received him. Tardiou reported to her the State Council's resolution on the state funeral. All dignitaries came to the Presidential Palace to sign condolences. The President of the Russian Youth Royalist Federation, Kachinbek, personally presented a condolence letter from Grand Duke Andrew of Russia, expressing the condolences of the former Russian royal family. Foreign representatives such as Chinese Chargé d'affaires Xie Weilin and Japanese Ambassador Nagaoka, all sent condolences to the French Foreign Minister. The Soviet Russian Ambassador visited the hospital yesterday and was very moved when he left. This morning, the Counselor of the Soviet Russian Embassy declared to reporters after offering condolences, "This kind of atrocious and foolish crime, how can the Soviet Russian Ambassador express his opinion on such a matter?" Condolence telegrams from heads of state and prime ministers of various countries are pouring in. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, Foreign Minister Grandi, and US Secretary of State Stimson all sent private telegrams of condolence. The Italian government also ordered all public institutions to fly flags at half-mast to express mourning.

Reuters London, 7th The British Chamberlain issued a notice on black-edged paper today, stating that the British court will wear mourning for a week to mourn the murdered French President Doumer. When Doumer is buried, the British Emperor will send the Prince as his representative to France to hold the rope.

Havas Geneva, 7th Today, the meetings of all the groups of the Disarmament Conference Committee were suspended to express mourning for President Doumer. The Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, and the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Drummond, sent telegrams to Tardiou in their personal names to express condolences. Newspapers all over the world unanimously expressed indignation at the news of Doumer's assassination and described the President's political career and his painful sacrifice for the country. Buerning sent a telegram of condolence on behalf of the German government. The whole of Germany flew flags at half-mast. When the news of Doumer's death was heard in London, the whole city mourned deeply. In addition to flying flags at half-mast, many hotels and banks in the city were surrounded by black gauze around the French flag. The public paid close attention to the attack, and everyone was talking about it in buses and subways. The churches also represented the faithful in expressing their deep sympathy.

Reuters Paris, 8th In the midst of the commotion after the assassination of President Doumer, a woman, dressed all in white, with an oriental physique and a solemn appearance, advanced among the startled men and women until she reached the former President, and knelt beside him, supporting his head with her arm, and used an embroidered towel to wipe the blood flowing from the wound. She was the daughter of an Annamese chieftain when Doumer was the Governor-General of Vietnam, and had always been protected by Doumer. It is said that Doumer's feelings for her were no different from those of a father to a daughter.

Former Japanese Ambassador to Russia Tanaka Inspects Eastern Provinces and Returns Home 90

Advocates Adding Consulates and Expanding Police Force

Denchu Agency Tokyo, 8th Because former Ambassador to Russia, Tanaka Tokichi, has inspected Manchuria and returned to Beijing, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs will review the locations in Manchuria where the ambassador proposed to establish new consulates within one or two days. The consulates that should be added are Dunhua, Tao'an, Jinzhou, Yimianpo, and Hailun; the branch offices are Ningguta and Fuyu. The expansion cost of the consulates in Manchuria is 1.5 million Japanese yen, and the expansion cost of the police in Manchuria is 5.8 million Japanese yen, totaling 8 million Japanese yen, which will be submitted to the extraordinary congress as a supplementary budget. Currently, it is being negotiated with the Ministry of Finance.

General Assembly of the Japanese Seiyukai 91

Faith in Japanese Party Politics Gradually Lost

Nationalist Movement Rises

Denchu Agency Tokyo, 8th The Kanto General Assembly of the first local assembly of the Seiyukai was held at Yokohama Park at 1:00 p.m. today. Prime Minister Inukai, Home Minister Suzuki, and Takushoku Minister Qin arrived in Yokohama at 11:00 a.m. After lunch, 25,000 local party members welcomed them to attend. First, Representative Nogata delivered the opening speech, followed by President Inukai, who gave a speech on the policies that should be implemented in the future. Then Secretary-General Mori gave a speech and decided on the following declaration: "The current cabinet of our party is devoting all its efforts to measures to address economic and national crises. The administration of the previous cabinet for three years only destroyed the national economy, so it cannot be rescued in a day or two. However, the current cabinet has reconvened the extraordinary congress to deal with measures to address the financial world, restore the general economy, and stabilize the people's lives. This declaration is hereby declared."

Japanese Allied Tokyo, 8th Prime Minister Inukai spoke at the Kanto General Assembly of the Seiyukai today, discussing the issue of China, saying that the war in Shanghai in the past three months has completely ended with the establishment of a ceasefire negotiation, and peace in that area has also been restored. The issue afterwards is how to effectively maintain the order of the international city of Shanghai. The result of the Shanghai incident this time did not harm Japan's national rights, but realized international coordination. As for Manchuria and Mongolia, with the establishment of a new country, order is also being restored. We firmly believe that the results of the League of Nations investigation team's visit to Manchuria will prove that Japan's self-defense actions since last year are based on the right path and are moving towards an ideal world step by step. That is, Manchuria and Shanghai are both brewing new atmospheres after the disturbances, and there is no doubt that it will have a good impact on all aspects. However, we cannot be satisfied with this, because we must fundamentally establish a good-neighborly policy with neighboring countries in order to achieve lasting peace.

Denchu Agency Tokyo, 8th The Japanese people's faith in party politics can be said to have fallen to the ground. The national essence movement has risen in response to the stimulation of the Manchurian Incident and the general trend overseas. Therefore, the establishment of new parties by Katsuma Akamatsu, Masago Nakano, etc., who broke away from the Social Democratic Party, and the Kokuhonsha of Hiranuma men, etc., with the military as the background, have all become rapidly apparent. These parties echo parts of the Seiyukai and the Minseito, so each political party feels very embarrassed and is struggling to find a way to deal with it. That is, the government's and the party's special committee for the revision of the election law also has to resist the national essence movement. Miki Bukichi of the Minseito also has contact with them. Therefore, the existing parties have formed a common front to consolidate their own parties, so the political world will fall into a state of confusion.

Russia Vigorously Promotes Electrification 94

National News Agency Moscow, 7th The All-Russian Electrification Congress opened here yesterday. The electrification program in the second five-year plan will be discussed in detail by famous electrical engineers and economists from all over the country under the leadership of the design committee Kupishev, and the methods will be determined next. It is expected that the country will generate 100 million kilowatt-hours of electricity by 1937, reaching the target at the end of the planned second five-year plan. According to current Soviet Russian authorities, several large power plants have been decided to be built, one of which is located on the Angara River in Siberia. It is expected that the electricity generated by the plant by hydropower will be three times the electricity generated by the hydropower of the Dnieprostrova and Volgastrova plants on the Volga River, so as to develop the industry in Siberia. According to the major plan for electrification in Russia, the first was originally formulated by Lenin in 1921, with the expectation of completion in ten years, but by 1931, its development status had far exceeded Lenin's original expectations, and there has been rapid progress since the implementation of the five-year plan.

Cliff Collapse on the Banks of the Rhone River 96

Lyon, France, 8th (Kuo Min News Agency) - This morning, a 190-foot cliff on the banks of the Rhone River here collapsed suddenly due to prolonged rain and underground hollowness, causing the complete collapse of a Western-style apartment building. The majority of the 53 residents were buried alive. At the same time, many gas pipes exploded, causing a large fire. Mayor Herriot, upon hearing the news, rushed to the scene with the Archbishop of Lyon to supervise the rescue efforts. However, by evening, only ten people had been rescued. It is estimated that at least thirty people have been crushed to death.

Chen Jitang Unifies Naval and Air Force Power 98

The First Army Group Headquarters Takes Over the Navy and Air Force

Guangzhou Special Dispatch - The brewing of the Southwest Government's reorganization and the Guangdong Provincial military authorities' prior takeover of the air force have been reported previously. The Guangdong air force was originally divided into the Zhongshan and Siyi factions. Chen Jitang of the First Army Group had already taken the Siyi faction into his own hands. Huang Guangrui, the first squadron leader's recent promotion to director of the aviation office, was a preparatory step to replace Zhang (Huichang). As a result, the Siyi (Taishan, Kaiping, etc.) faction's power has surged in the air force in recent years. Therefore, the authorities' sudden abolition of the Air Force General Headquarters and the removal of Zhang Huichang's position did not cause major internal problems. It is reported that after Huang Guangrui was ordered to serve as Air Force Commander, he immediately closed the old Air Force General Headquarters and reorganized the Air Force Headquarters, which is now directly under the First Army Group Headquarters. The Air Force Headquarters established by Huang Guangrui is slightly smaller in scale than before. The personnel for the various positions in the headquarters have also been internally determined, with Hu Jinya appointed as Chief of Staff, Guan Liuting as Chief Secretary, Hu Jixian as Director of the Military Affairs Department, Huang Qibin as Director of the Adjutant Department, Chen Xiu as Director of the Technical Department, Liu Zhiyan as Director of the Navigation Department, Yang Guanyu continuing to serve as Principal of the Aviation School, Zhang Zixuan as Commander of the Aviation Guard Regiment, Deng Yueming as Director of the Air Force Flying Training Team, Mei Long'an continuing to serve as Director of the Aircraft Factory, Tan Shou as Captain of the First Aircraft Squadron, Ding Jixu continuing as Captain of the Second Squadron, Zhou Bocheng as Captain of the Third Squadron, Xie Mang as Captain of the Fourth Squadron, and Wu Jianwen as Captain of the Fifth Squadron. Recently, it is also planned to establish a Sixth Squadron with six locally-made "Yangcheng" aircraft. After the First Army Group Headquarters resolved the air force issue, but because the leaders of the air force and navy had close relations on weekdays, Navy Commander Chen Ce hurriedly left the province for Hong Kong on the day the air force issue was resolved. The navy's offshore fleet, such as the Feiying, Zhongshan, Zhixin, and Yingrui, suddenly concentrated on Hainan Island, while the river defense ships, such as the Jiangong, Jianggu, Guanghua, and Long Jun, sailed to Tangjiawan. Only a few shallow-water vessels were moored in the provincial river. On the morning of the 2nd, important officials of the Navy General Headquarters did not go to the office. Chief of Staff Chen Ding and Marine Corps Commander Chen Qingyun had already gone to Hong Kong. Therefore, the First Army Group Headquarters decided to resolve the navy issue as well. It immediately ordered the Humen Fortress and the Changzhou Yuzhu Forts to use force to prevent the ships in the provincial river from exiting. On the 3rd, the Southwest Political Affairs Committee of the National Government decided to abolish the Navy First Fleet Headquarters. The original navy was placed under the jurisdiction of the First Army Group, and Chen Ce was transferred to be a Senior Advisor to the First Army Group. (Note: On the same day, it was also decided to abolish the Air Force General Headquarters. The original air force was placed under the jurisdiction of the First Army Group, Zhang Huichang was transferred to be a Senior Advisor to the First Army Group, and Huang Guangrui was appointed as Acting Air Force Commander of the First Army Group.) Upon investigation, the navy's internal members had shared hardships with Chen Ce for a long time and were very united, unlike the air force's internal members, who were easier to divide. Therefore, after Chen Ce left his post, the ships acted freely. Even the four small ships moored in the provincial river, such as the Haihu, Guanggeng, Guangjin, and Anbei, rekindled their fires on the morning of the 3rd, wanting to sail out of Humen. The Humen Fortress used flags to stop them, but they did not listen, so they opened fire. The garrison troops were then dispatched on armed ships to intercept them. The four ships, facing the fortress's strong defense, returned to the river near Huangpu. The captain of the Guangjin was detained. On the afternoon of the 3rd, the First Army Group Headquarters sent Navy veteran Zhao Guizhang to recover the Guangjin. The rest were not obtained. On the evening of the 3rd, faint gunfire was heard, suggesting that they were still in a standoff. At four o'clock in the afternoon of the 4th, the First Army Group Headquarters sent Military Affairs Director Wen Zhongcheng to the Navy Headquarters to take over the documents. At that time, most of the old staff had already left. Chen Di came out to negotiate. Wen completed the takeover of the Navy Department that afternoon. (May 4th)

Robbery on the Jinpu Railway 99

Jinan Correspondence - At three o'clock this morning, the Jinpu No. 9 train, traveling to a place three or four li north of Anlingzhen Station, suddenly a shot rang out on the train. More than ten bandits were discovered inside the train. One party boarded the locomotive and ordered the driver to stop the train. The other party confiscated the guns of the three security guards escorting the train (the three had a total of two guns). They then began to rob passengers of their money. The train was a slow train traveling between Tianjin and Jinan. Most of the passengers were poor and did not have much money. Even one yuan and eight jiao were completely searched. They did not take clothes. After about half an hour, the search was completed, and they got off the train, whistled, and left. The passengers on the train were greatly frightened. The train arrived in Jinan one hour late. According to people on the train, when the train arrived at Lianzhen, more than ten people bought tickets and boarded the train. The robbers were the people who boarded at Lianzhen. Later, the No. 201 Pingpu through train heard the alert when it arrived at Lianzhen. Because it was night, it did not dare to depart and waited until dawn before heading south. It was originally scheduled to arrive in Jinan at nine o'clock in the morning, but it did not arrive until 10:15, it is said.

Feng Yong Passes Through Jinan on His Way Back to Ping 100

Leading 120 Student Volunteers

Jinan Correspondence - Feng Yong, the president of Feng Yong University, after the Shanghai Incident, led the student volunteer army organized by the university to the front line of Liuhe to participate in the battle. Now that the Shanghai battle has stopped, he led 120 student volunteers from the university to take the Jinpu No. 2 train at ten o'clock this morning, passing through Jinan on his way back to Ping. The Jinpu Railway specially provided three carriages for free transportation. After arriving in Jinan, they immediately formed a team and got off the train, singing military songs. They went to the open space east of the platform to drill. They were all in yellow military uniforms, including seven female students, who were also fully armed, acting as vanguards, in shorts that exposed their knees, strong and powerful, and almost indistinguishable from men. According to Feng, the army suffered more than ten casualties while working on the front line. Today, there are a total of 120 people. When they arrived at the front line, they first patrolled the Liuhe area, and then went to Changshu, Kunshan, and Suzhou to direct soldiers to dig trenches. Recently, because the war has stopped and a peace conference is about to be held, the army is returning to Ping for training. He will still return to the front line in the coming days. When asked how he felt about leading the volunteer army to participate in the battle this time, Feng said that he felt that China's current situation is still unable to cooperate. The government and the people still cannot understand each other. If this continues, he fears that there will be a second and third Shanghai Incident in the future. If we do not seek unity, not only will Japan invade, but other countries will also follow suit. He hopes that the whole country will wake up, quickly seek cooperation, and jointly resist foreign aggression. The lessons of the Jinan May 3rd Massacre are a good example. He especially hopes that everyone will pay attention and do their best to promote it so that the public understands the current national crisis and rises up to become strong. Now, the Shanghai public and student representatives have injured Guo Taiqi, which is said to be because he signed a treaty that lost rights and humiliated the country. However, he said that such actions are inevitably too superficial. He also said that some of his team members are still staying in Taicang and Kunshan. Feng asked about the situation in Shandong and whether Chairman Han was in Jinan. The reporter replied that the area was peaceful and Han was in Jinan. At 9:45, Feng led the army to board the train and headed north on the original train at 10 o'clock. (5th)

The Situation in Fujian After the Communists Invaded Zhangzhou 101

Guangzhou Correspondence - Various associations and organizations in the capital of Fujian Province, due to the rampant banditry in the province, recently sent Wu Huqin as a representative to Guangdong to discuss with the provincial military authorities the dispatch of troops to Fujian to suppress the spread. The reporter, considering the dangerous situation of the banditry in Fujian Province, visited Representative Wu yesterday to inquire about everything. He was kind enough to provide detailed information. Here is a summary of what Wu said:

The Communist Party's Intentions - During the large-scale campaign by the Guangdong army into Jiangxi to suppress the bandits, the bandits in that area fled from southern Jiangxi to Fujian. They then joined forces with the Fujian bandits and attacked Longyan. The purpose of this move was to seize Zhangzhou as a base, with the intention of invading Fuzhou and Xiamen to secure a sea route. Therefore, after capturing Longyan, they went straight to Zhangzhou. Their intention is obvious. Those who invaded Zhangzhou this time were the rebel army of Sun Lianzhong, Ji Zhendong's troops, and Luo Bingyao, Lin Biao, and You Ruixuan's troops under Peng Huaide, totaling more than 10,000 people. After occupying Zhangzhou, the bandits intended to attack Xiamen with all their strength. However, because Xiamen was heavily defended, they failed. They then turned to Tong'an to attack, intending to attack Fuzhou.

Defense and Suppression Situation - When the bandits attacked Longyan on the 10th of last month, the troops stationed there were Yang Fengnian's troops of the First Brigade under Zhang Zhen's 49th Division of the Fujian Defense Army. The brigade was suddenly besieged by the bandits, broke out of the encirclement, and retreated to Shizhong, and then to Nanjing and Zhangzhou. Because Nanjing had defenses and Zhangzhou was guarded by Wang Chengyun's troops of the Second Brigade under Zhang Zhen, the bandits' momentum, although fierce, was not easy to predict. However, because the divisions did not dare to engage the bandits, they retreated on their own, resulting in both places being occupied by the bandits. After Zhang Zhen withdrew from Zhangzhou, he retreated to Tong'an. The bandits have continued to advance towards Tong'an, and Tong'an is in imminent danger. As for Xiamen, the Zhangxia Garrison Commander Lin Guogeng is now leading the naval garrison troops to defend it closely, so there is probably no need to worry. Recently, Fang Shengtao of the Provincial Government, in order to plan for the suppression campaign due to the rampant banditry, rushed back to Fuzhou from Beijing. He then, together with Chen Jiliang, commander of the First Fleet of the Navy, took the Chu You and Chu Tong ships to Xiamen to oversee the situation.

Current Situation in Fujian - After the bandits captured Longyan and continued to occupy Zhangzhou, Xiamen, because it is close to Zhangzhou, was in a state of panic and extreme shock. At present, because the defense is tight and the bandits cannot succeed, the situation in Xiamen seems to be slightly stable. However, the bandits have turned to attack Tong'an, and the situation is very critical. Chairman Fang, upon receiving the report, immediately ordered the troops stationed from Tong'an to Fuzhou to defend closely to prevent them from being infiltrated. At present, in addition to the Zhang Zhen Division stationed in Tong'an, Chen Guohui of the First Brigade of the Provincial Defense and He Xianzhu of the 8th Defense Zone Bandit Suppression Command are stationed in the Quanzhou, Yongchun, and Xinghua areas above Tong'an. In the Fuzhou provincial capital, the troops of the 56th National Defense Division Liu Heding, the troops of the First Brigade of the Marine Corps Yang Tingying, and the entire Second Mixed Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army Xiao Shuxuan are jointly defending. As for Yanping, Jianning, Shaowu, and other areas in northern Fujian, the troops of the 56th National Defense Division Liu Heding, the Provisional Second Division Lu Xingbang, and the Independent Brigade Zhou Zhiqun were originally stationed there and could provide support. However, due to traffic blockages, they can only defend themselves strictly at present. Commander Liu Heding, in order to consolidate the defense of that area, moved the headquarters of the 56th Division from Fuzhou to Yanping to facilitate command. At present, in addition to the strict defense by the stationed troops in various parts of Fujian Province, they are also urging Commander-in-Chief Chen to send a large army to Fujian to urgently attack Longyan from Shanghang and Yongding, so as to cut off the bandits' connection, making it easier to suppress them in one fell swoop and eliminate future troubles. (Far East News Agency)

Anhui Province Rushes to Build Provincial Highways 102

The Military Commission Sets a Deadline for the Completion of the Anhui-Zhejiang Road

Wuhu Correspondence - After the establishment of the new government in Anhui Province, it announced the policy of governing Anhui. In addition to pacification and financial management, it was to complete the provincial highways with all its strength. It was also resolved to use 600,000 yuan from the Anhui rice surtax as a special fund for road construction. However, recently, due to the small amount of rice exports, the income from the surtax is slow to meet the urgent needs. It was decided to use the rice surtax as collateral and borrow 600,000 yuan from Anhui merchants in Shanghai. Construction Director Cheng Zhenjun has gone to Shanghai to negotiate. This loan is specifically for the construction of the Tunxi-Changhua Road. This road can connect the traffic between Zhejiang and Anhui provinces and is related to military transportation. The Construction Department recently received a telegram from the Transportation Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs, stating that the long-distance bus route from Guangde via Xuancheng to Wuhu should be completed as soon as possible, as instructed by Chairman Jiang of the Military Commission, and the deadline should not exceed May. The provincial government immediately telegraphed the governments of Wuhu, Xuancheng, and Guangde counties to start raising funds and recruiting workers immediately, and appointed Duan Tianjue and Chen Jiarui as engineers and supervisors to supervise the construction in various counties. The total cost of labor and materials is about 300,000 yuan. It will take until the beginning of June at the earliest to complete the entire project. (5th)

Anhui Provincial Government Reaffirms the Opium Prohibition Order 103

But in Fact, Public Sale of Opium

Bengbu Correspondence - The opium disaster in Anhui Province has been poisoning the area for many years. The authorities have always used the excuse of "prohibiting opium through taxation," but the result has only increased opium poisoning, causing more harm. Sometimes they collect opium taxes on the one hand and strictly prohibit it on the other, which is self-contradictory, leaving the people at a loss. For example, in the winter of last year, when the Anhui Special Taxation Office was strictly collecting seedling taxes from various counties, the former Civil Affairs Director Liu Fu issued a vernacular announcement, strictly prohibiting planting. Currently, the southern and northern Anhui special taxation offices are still implementing the public sale of opium. The new Civil Affairs Director Luo Liangjian has also issued a strict opium prohibition order. The official rhetoric is contradictory as before. The full text of Luo Liangjian's instructions to the sixty counties of the province and the public security bureaus on land and water is recorded below to show a glimpse: "It has been found that opium prohibition is one of the important policies of the political training period. The Opium Prohibition Committee has repeatedly ordered us to follow the rules for the implementation of the opium prohibition law, and to investigate and prohibit planting, transportation, sale, and smoking separately. Since the beginning of my tenure, I have visited and investigated the opium prohibition situation in Anhui Province. It is inevitable that it is becoming increasingly lax. The county and bureau chiefs, who are in charge of the local area, have the special responsibility of prohibiting opium. If this continues for a long time, it will be difficult to excuse them for their negligence. Therefore, I hereby reaffirm the opium prohibition order. In the future, those responsible for opium prohibition must work hard to implement it in order to eradicate the accumulated poison. If there are still those who despise the law and fail to handle it effectively, or who are outwardly compliant but inwardly resistant and perfunctory, once discovered, they will be severely punished according to the law and will not be lenient. In addition to separate orders, it is hereby ordered that the county and bureau chiefs comply and order their subordinates to comply as well." However, it is not known whether this circular will be effective. (May 3rd)

Resolution of the Jinpu Railway Corruption Case 104

Overweight Transportation of Bengbu Red Grain

Merchants Voluntarily Accept Punishment

The Jinpu Railway Northern Section staff recently discovered a suspected corruption case. According to the railway bureau's investigation, it was related to the overweight transportation of Bengbu red grain from Tianjin to Cangzhou and other stations. Upon discovering this, the railway bureau immediately ordered the transportation department to investigate the matter strictly. It summoned nineteen suspected employees to the bureau and, for the sake of caution, immediately organized a hearing committee to investigate thoroughly. On the one hand, it also sent additional personnel to investigate secretly. According to the results of the hearing and investigation, the overweight transportation of red grain this time was purely because small-scale merchants colluded with porters and the freight handlers of the transport company to secretly load it onto the train, hoping to transport it for free. The responsibility for the overweight is still borne by the company. Now the companies are voluntarily accepting punishment. The bureau believes that although the employees did not engage in corruption, they did not notice it at the time, and they are difficult to excuse for negligence in their duties. It is said that they have been punished according to the severity of their circumstances and have been instructed to supervise and strictly check the loading and transportation of goods in the future to prevent abuses. The bureau has also reported the occurrence and handling of this case to the Ministry of Railways.

Local Correspondence

Jiangyin 105

Water Police Seize Boats Smuggling Rice - Jiangyin suffered a famine last year, and this year farmers in various villages are rioting and seizing rice. Since the Shanghai Incident, there have been unscrupulous merchants smuggling supplies to the enemy, often shipping them to Chongming to pass enemy ships. Several cases have been cracked down, but they were all vaguely dealt with leniently. Recently, a wealthy merchant in Wuxi has acted as a traitor, smuggling rice, exporting it through Changshu and Jiangyin, and colluding with powerful smugglers in the two counties. Changshu intercepted hundreds of dan and reported to the province for instructions, but no action has been taken. At Huangtiangang, Jiangyin, on the afternoon of the 3rd, Zhao Yunlin, a patrol officer of the 2nd Squadron of the Water Police, seized seven or eight hundred [units] of japonica rice. After inspection, it was reported to the county party department. According to the boatmen, it was purchased by Yufengtai Rice Store in Taixian and transported to Xichuan. There were a total of 2,500 shi. This was the first batch, and the rest will be shipped later. After being verified by the standing committee member Zhang Erjie's phone call to Magistrate Ma, and the business association's standing committee member Yin Zhaoyong held a certificate, they were released. According to the water police, in recent days, more than 4,000 shi of white rice, coarse rice, japonica rice, and indica rice have been exported through the port.

Nantong 106

Change of Leader of the Salt Affairs Tax Police Team - Su Tiehan, the leader of the Huainan Salt Affairs Tax Police Brigade stationed in Tonghai, such as Rugao County, has been replaced by the Salt Affairs Audit Office and replaced by Shao Shaoying.

Soaring Rice Prices and the Opening of Affordable Rice Sales - Nantong's rice prices have recently soared, reaching 18 yuan per shi. The county government has requested the Food Management Committee to find ways to stabilize prices. In the four townships, there is a famine. Each district has opened affordable rice sales and distributed sweet potato chips to relieve the famine.

Jiangbei Cattle Dealers are Very Active - In the counties north of the Yangtze River, cattle dealers have recently been collecting cattle in large quantities and secretly exporting them through the small ports of Nantong. On the 7th, during the high tide at Xiaoligang, 34 cattle were intercepted at night. The cattle dealer Shan Bu'ao was sent to the county government for interrogation.

Yangzhou 107

Robbery and Injury Case at Huanghualing - The county government, according to Guo Zhaoqi, the head of the 7th Autonomous District, reported that the families of Li Zhaogeng and Li Chunpeng, residents of three villages in Huanghualing, were attacked on the same day by more than 20 bandits who rushed into their gates, searched and looted everything, burned Li Chunpeng, and beat Li Zhaoguang and his two daughters-in-law, injuring four people. Two six-year-old boys from each family were taken away. He begged the county government to arrest the bandits and rescue the hostages. Because neither the plaintiff nor the public security bureau in charge had reported the matter, the county government ordered the public security bureau to investigate, fill out a form, and report it. At the same time, it instructed the police team to investigate and arrest the stolen goods and try to rescue the hostages.

Gaoyou 108

Communists Rampant in Anhui - A large group of bandits suddenly occupied the place of Ma Gang in Xuyi County, Anhui Province, the other day. They burned, looted, and did whatever they wanted. All the pillboxes in Dongyang City were burned down. It is said that the bandits have now spread to Tianchang and Tongchengzhen, and are fighting fiercely with the Anhui Provincial Independent Regiment, the militia, and the defense forces of Tian and Xu counties. One company of the Independent Regiment was disarmed, and more than 20 members of the militia and the defense forces of Tian and Xu counties were killed or injured. The government forces were defeated and retreated to the encirclement. The situation is critical. It is reported that the communist leaders Qi Wanbei, Mei Yichong, Li Lianfang, and Zhang Baifei are directing the bandits internally. The villages they pass through are burned and killed. The residents of nearby villages have fled. It is said that the government forces have telegraphed the Anhui provincial government for help. Shen Qi, the captain of the 1st squadron of police stationed at the Ta'erji in this county, is afraid that the bandits will enter the borders of Gaoyou, and has come to the city to ask for instructions. It is said that Magistrate Li is planning to send heavy troops to defend the area.

Bandits Rob a Fishing Boat, One Person Dies - Zhu Chenglin and Ju Jinbang, fishermen from Minjiaqiao Town, north of the county, sold a boatload of fish in the Qingzhen Township of the 11th district the other day. The boat was moored at the Laoyata Wharf. Zhu Chenglin went to various villages to sell fish, but he met rain on the way and could not return to the boat, so he stayed at the home of his relative Yuan Baoxing. Ju Jinbang was guarding the fishing boat alone. Unexpectedly, at two o'clock in the night, two lake bandits suddenly came with broadswords and boarded the boat to search and loot. Because they found nothing, they tied up Chenglin with ropes and threw him into the river. The bandits then pushed the boat away. When Zhu Chenglin returned, he only saw Ju's corpse floating on the water. He is now planning to report the case to the city and ask the county government to arrest the bandits strictly.

Jiaxing 109

Deserters from Haiyan Intercepted One After Another - Five squad leaders from the 9th company of the [unclear number] battalion of the 496th regiment of the 249th brigade of the 83rd division stationed near Shendang Town in Haiyan were incited by bandits in Taihu and, at midnight on the 1st, colluded with platoon leaders Wei Ting and Yang Fuquan and 40 soldiers, carrying 36 guns, and fled from Shendang to Wangdian. The division headquarters discovered this and sent teams to pursue them in different directions, and telegraphed the Provincial Security Department and the public security bureaus of various counties to intercept them. Eight deserters have now been killed and 36 captured, and 31 guns have been seized. The rest abandoned their weapons, disguised themselves, and fled. Yesterday, Division Commander Jiang Fusheng telegraphed Chairman Lu to seize them.

Xuzhou 110

Methods for Relief of Flood Victims in Xubu - In addition to the Xubu flood relief association and the Red Swastika Society raising funds for relief, the Jinpu Garrison Command strictly ordered the administrative authorities to find ways to provide relief and send people away. However, during the spring famine, the number of flood victims is still increasing. Although there are flood relief associations, Red Swastika Societies, etc., that purchase and transport flour at affordable prices, and private individuals provide porridge and cakes for relief, most of the relief is concentrated in the urban area, and there is little regard for the countryside. A month ago, the flood relief association suggested lending money to help rural people with farming. County Magistrate Yang Weinong, Hu Yunqing of the flood relief association, and Xu Jianqing went to various districts to borrow money from wealthy households. It was stipulated that the loan for a large district would be 9,000 yuan, a medium district 8,000 yuan, and a small district 7,000 yuan. The total number of districts in the county is twelve. About 100,000 yuan has been raised in one week, which will be distributed to various districts. However, it is just a drop in the bucket and is difficult to benefit all the victims. Those who are thin and haggard still cannot disappear from the streets.

Joint Meeting of the Bar Association's Executive and Supervisory Committees 111

106th Meeting

The Shanghai Bar Association convened its 106th joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees yesterday (Sunday). The following committee members attended: Shen Junru, Yan Yinwu, Shi Liang, Yang Zhihao, Jiang Yiping, Lu Dingkui, Tang Hao, Zhu Fujiu, Jiang Jiemin, Chen Tingrui, Zhang Zhirang, Zhang Zhengxue, Wu Jingxiong, etc. Shen Junru was elected as chairman, and Dai Jixian recorded the minutes. The proposed motions are recorded as follows: (1) Report from the Standing Committee regarding the arrest of Ahn Chang-ho, a Korean who had become a Chinese citizen, by the French Concession Police. He was handed over to the Japanese military authorities without being brought before the court. Telegrams were sent to both the Ministry of Justice and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting investigation and protest. A motion for ratification was proposed and passed. (2) A motion from the Sino-Korean Anti-Japanese Grand Alliance requesting serious protest and a telegram to the League of Nations to seek intervention and prevent the French Concession police from arbitrarily arresting Korean political prisoners and extraditing them to Japan, thereby undermining Chinese legal authority. (3) A motion from citizen Mr. Qiu requesting serious protest against the French Concession police for disregarding the law, intruding into homes without cause for searches, and disturbing the peace. (4) A motion from member Wu Mai stating that the French Concession police arbitrarily arrested Korean political prisoners without bringing them before the court and extradited them directly. He requested that the Chinese delegate to the League of Nations be notified to submit a report and urge the Japanese side to pay attention. Furthermore, he requested that all major bar associations and renowned legal scholars in various countries be notified to jointly condemn the misconduct of the French Consulate. The above three motions were combined and resolved that a declaration should be issued on legal grounds regarding the French Concession police's arbitrary arrest of Korean political prisoners, which set an international precedent. The drafting of the declaration was entrusted to the Standing Committee members and Committee Member Chen Tingrui jointly. (5) A letter from the Shanghai District Court Prosecutor's Office replying regarding the case of lawyer Wu Mai being illegally detained and injured by the Municipal Public Security Bureau, stating that it had been forwarded to the Jiangsu High Court for review and had now been instructed to transfer it to the Criminal Court for handling. It was resolved to notify member Wu Mai for his information. (6) A letter from member Lu Jianai responding that the accusation of fraudulent acquisition of property was not factual. Furthermore, Gao Xinglang, the father of the original informant, came to the meeting to explain. Standing Committee member Lu Dingkui also reported that Gao Xinglang came to the meeting to explain the situation and presented a signed statement. It was resolved that since the father of the original informant had stated that the accusation was not factual, the matter should be dropped. (7) A letter from member Liu Shifang forwarding translated Chinese documents and requesting discussion of points that were difficult to authenticate. It was resolved to forward it to the Chongming County Government for investigation. (8) A letter from member Gu Kenfu responding that lawyer Yao Tingguang violated the resolution by handling cases for Japanese individuals and instigating insults and abuse of the parties involved. The facts were clear, and he requested that the matter be promptly addressed to maintain discipline. It was resolved to copy the original letter and forward it to member Yao Tingguang for a factual response. (9) Member Huang Han reported on the review of Wang Xingsheng's complaint against lawyer Yang Changchi for accepting representation from both parties, requesting discussion. It was resolved that since it was found that member Yang Changchi had not accepted representation from both parties, the matter should be dropped, and the original document should be filed. (10) The Economic Committee returned the referral of two motions from the Shanghai Various Organizations National Salvation Joint Council regarding the development of national salvation work, hoping for donations for operational expenses, and requesting donations for military supplies for the 47th Division, stating that the donations had already been designated for a specific purpose and requesting that other means be found. It was resolved to return it to the Economic Committee for reconsideration. (11) Members Zhou Boang, Pan Zhensheng, Shen Xiaoxiang, Fang Zhong, Huang Jue, and Zhuang Chengyi, respectively, responded that they were willing to serve as volunteer legal advisors to the French Concession Rent Reduction Association and requested referral. It was resolved to send a letter to the French Concession Rent Reduction Association for its information. (12) Member Chen Zhaoqi sent a letter requesting that the legal ambiguity regarding the conflict between Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the Petition Law and Executive Yuan Directive No. 4522 be forwarded for interpretation. (13) Member Lu Fubao sent a letter requesting that it be forwarded for interpretation as to whether being appointed as a legal advisor constitutes practicing as a lawyer. (13) Member Liu Shifang sent a letter requesting that legal ambiguities in the Administrative Litigation Law be forwarded for interpretation. The above three motions were combined and resolved to forward replies to the respective members for their information, based on the Jiangsu High Court's repeated instructions not to provide interpretations. (14) A letter from the Zhenjiang Bar Association requesting that 200 copies of the eighth supplementary regulations be printed. It was resolved to send a letter to the association stating that after the book is published, they can purchase it at cost. (15) A letter from the Hankou Bar Association stating that it had not sent a general report to the Lawyers Association and that the party department had rejected its registration. It was resolved to file the letter. (16) Citizen Liang Jiayou reported that lawyer Yao Xichen helped the landlord oppress the tenant and requested that the lawyer be notified not to accept the case. It was resolved to file the report. (17) The Shanghai Postal Workers' Union and the Postal Workers' Union requested assistance in advocating for a plan to consolidate the postal base, temporarily maintain existing postal rates, and reduce the burden on the people. It was resolved to file the request. (18) The Shanghai Various Organizations Memorial Service for Anti-Japanese Martyrs and Victims requested that willing organizations elect representatives to jointly initiate the event. It was resolved to file the request. (19) The Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association requested that donations be collected on their behalf. It was resolved to reply to the association that it would be done. (20) Lawyers Li Zhaofu, Xu Jinyu, Sha Qianli, etc. applied for membership. It was resolved to approve the applications. The meeting adjourned.

Two Committees for Silkworm Cocoon Industry Relief Officially Begin Work Today 112

Registration of Old Factory Silk and Old Cocoons Limited to a Specific Time

Government First Allocates 2 Million Taels in Assistance Funds

Cocoon Prices Set to Protect Cocoon Merchants as Much as Possible

The Committee for Reorganizing Old Factory Silk and Old Cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and the Committee for Promoting Sales of Existing Factory Silk in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, officially begin work today, after the government appointed the committee members and announced the establishment. Registration of old silk and cocoons is limited to a specific time, and cocoon collection methods have been set. Details of the various items are recorded separately below:

Official Operation　The Committee for Reorganizing Old Factory Silk and Old Cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang and the Committee for Promoting Sales of Existing Factory Silk in Jiangsu and Zhejiang have set up offices on the third floor of No. 15, Museum Road. Yesterday, preparations were completed, and it was decided to officially begin work today, from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM and from 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM. Registration of old factory silk and old cocoons mortgaged by various factories will be handled starting today. The deadline for local areas is before May 15th, and the deadline for outside areas is before May 20th. Staff will be dispatched for inspection and weighing, and certificates will be issued.

Cocoon Collection Organization　The government has already allocated 2 million taels in subsidies for old factory silk and factory silk reeled from old cocoons. It is stipulated that a subsidy of 100 taels per shipment will be provided for the transportation and export of raw silk and that the raw silk export tax and the silk industry public debt fund surcharge will be suspended. As for the issue of cocoon collection this spring, organizations of silk and cocoon merchants and gentry from various regions will borrow money from silver shops and banks to handle cocoon collection matters. It has been decided to stop issuing 10 million yuan in cocoon collection exchange vouchers. It is reported that Shaoxing, Shengxian, Yuyao, Jiaxing, Haining, Huzhou, and other places in Zhejiang have already been organized. New cocoons will soon be on the market. Wuxi, Suzhou, and other places in Jiangsu are also actively preparing organizations because the arrival of their new cocoons will be slightly later than in Zhejiang.

Cocoon Price Regulations　Zeng Yangfu, Director of the Zhejiang Department of Industry, and He Yushu, Director of the Jiangsu Department of Industry, have been in Shanghai for several days, discussing the new cocoon collection price with the two committees. If calculated according to the current silk price of 500 taels per picul, the cocoon price should be at least 350 taels, but the collection price is only around 20 yuan. In order to take into account the livelihood of farmers and the difficulties of silk factories, it has been decided to adopt a fair and equitable compromise. The price of improved varieties of cocoons will be as high as 35 yuan per picul and as low as 20 yuan. The price of Du varieties of cocoons will be as high as 25 yuan per picul and as low as 15 yuan. The governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces will issue announcements to cocoon collection agencies in various regions to comply with this uniformly.

Government Protection　After cocoons are listed in various regions, the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have decided to assume full responsibility for protecting cocoon collection and ensuring the smooth transportation of cocoons. They will also try their best to restore transportation. Zeng Yangfu, Director of the Zhejiang Department of Industry, took the Shanghai-Hangzhou train back to Hangzhou the day before yesterday. He Yushu, Director of the Jiangsu Department of Industry, is also scheduled to return to Zhenjiang by boat today. Both are actively preparing for protection matters. Therefore, there is no need to worry about the public security of cocoon collection this spring.

Former Acting Chairman of Hunan Province, Zhang Yipeng, Accused 113

Of Owning a Large Sum of Money to a Hardware Store in Changsha

Using the Promise of Securing the Position of Chief of Public Security as Bait

Resulting in Neither the Position nor the Repayment of the Debt

The Son of the Creditor Files a Criminal Lawsuit

Zhang Yipeng, a native of Hunan, was appointed as the acting chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government in the 16th year of the Republic of China after the National Revolutionary Army marched north and recovered the two Hunan provinces. However, he still owed a large sum of money to the Baiji Hardware Store in Changsha from before. Wu Lishan, the manager of the store, believed that since Zhang had been appointed as the chairman, the old debt should naturally be repaid, so he went to demand payment. Zhang initially agreed to repay in installments, and then promised to introduce Wu to fill

The Position of Chief of Public Security in Hankou,　but the result was nothing more than empty promises. By the end of Zhang's term, he still had not received a single cent. Later, the owner of the store, Cheng Linpu, and Wu Lishan both passed away one after another. Zhang completely forgot about this debt. Recently, Cheng Daode, the son of Cheng Linpu, learned that Zhang had taken his family to Shanghai and was residing in room 124 of Jing'an Villa on Jing'an Temple Road.

Therefore, He Also Followed to Shanghai,　lodging at the Wanshun Inn at No. 15, Xin Kaihe Road. He then hired a lawyer to send a letter to Zhang demanding payment, but with no results. Therefore, he further hired lawyer Xi Yafu to file a private criminal lawsuit against Zhang Yipeng and his wife with the First Special District Court, requesting that they be punished for embezzlement and ordered to repay the money. The original complaint briefly stated that the plaintiff's late father, Cheng Linpu, opened the Baiji Hardware Store in Changsha. Between the 10th and 11th years of the Republic of China, the first defendant (i.e., Zhang Yipeng) contracted for the Hunan Mint and continuously obtained

Silver Advances from the Plaintiff's Late Father,　totaling 22,217.352 taels of silver according to the passbook and 20,251.972 taels of silver according to the vouchers. In September of the 11th year, the first defendant subcontracted the Hunan Mint to a Mr. Zhao and delivered 3,911 yuan in foreign currency (equivalent to 2,834 taels of silver) to the plaintiff's late father for the voucher. The remaining money was to be transferred by Mr. Zhao to the defendant for delivery. However, the first defendant delivered the money that should have been delivered to the second defendant (i.e., Zhang's wife),

Consuming the Money Completely　and refusing to hand it over. Later, Wu Lishan, the manager of the Baiji Hardware Store, repeatedly demanded payment, but he was always met with perfunctory responses. In the 16th year, the defendant served as the acting chairman of the Hunan Provincial Government. Manager Wu Lishan demanded payment several times, as the debt had been outstanding for a long time. The first and second defendants both agreed to repay in installments. However, the defendants were untrustworthy, on the one hand making empty promises and on the other hand even

Using Political Tactics　promising to introduce Manager Wu Lishan as the chief of the Hankou Public Security Bureau, in order to deal with him perfunctorily, resulting in the long-standing unresolved case. In the winter of that year, Manager Wu Lishan passed away due to illness, and the Baiji Hardware Store also suffered huge losses, resulting in its closure. The plaintiff's late father, Cheng Linpu, also died of anger. Now the defendant has fled to Shanghai and is hiding in the jurisdiction, so he has specially presented the defendant's embezzlement situation to the court, requesting that the defendant be arrested and punished according to Article 356 of the Criminal Law

With the Deserved Punishment,　and that the defendants be ordered to jointly repay the plaintiff the embezzled sum of 39,635.324 taels of silver, which would be a matter of public convenience. The case was heard yesterday by Qiao Wanxuan, a judge of the Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Because the defendants Zhang Yipeng and his wife both failed to appear for questioning, it could not proceed. Judge Qiao then ordered a further summons for the defendants to appear for questioning.

The People's Livelihood Improvement Society Held Its Inaugural Meeting Yesterday 114

The People's Livelihood Improvement Society has gained social recognition since its inception and organization. Yesterday at 2:00 PM, the society held its inaugural meeting at No. 20, Museum Road. Dozens of members attended, including Zhu Maocheng, Li Denghui, Ying Shugui, Hu Shuhua, Li Zhaohuan, Zhong Ketuo, Liu Zhanen, Huang Jingwan, Yu Qingtang, Chen Binhe, Zheng Wenhan, etc. Zhu Maocheng was elected as chairman, and Jiang Yingsheng recorded the minutes, passing the society's constitution. The society's current propositions are roughly as follows: (1) All facilities of the state and society should aim at the happiness of the people. (2) The state and national economic construction should have a comprehensive and rational plan and organization. (3) Production and distribution enterprises should be socialized and cooperative. (4) National education should be completed within a specified period and designated educational funds should not be used for other purposes. (5) Central and local education funds should be at least equal to military expenditures. (6) The central and local governments should do their best to organize public welfare facilities and support various undertakings beneficial to the people's livelihood.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Convenes the Third Congress 115

Soliciting Proposals from Members Starting Today

Membership Application Suspended One Month Before the Meeting

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued an announcement regarding the convocation of the third member congress, stating that Article 39, Paragraph 1 of the chamber's constitution stipulates that the member congress shall be held regularly in June of each year, and Article 24 stipulates that the term of office for executive committee members and supervisory committee members shall be four years, with half being re-elected every two years, and Article 25 stipulates that the term of office for the chairman and standing committee members shall be two years. The date of this congress and the re-election of terms are all stipulated, and should be complied with accordingly. Therefore, as proposed by the 91st standing committee meeting and passed by the 24th executive committee meeting, the third member congress will be convened at 9:00 AM on June 18th, and the re-election will be held at the same time. In accordance with the provisions of Articles 16 and 46 of the constitution, the period from May 9th to June 8th will be for members to re-elect representatives and for the chamber to collect membership fees and solicit proposals. After May 18th and before June 18th, new membership applications will be suspended. In addition to sending separate notices with the representative registration list, members should submit the representative registration list, membership fees, and three-tenths of the public debt fund, as well as proposals to be submitted to the congress, to the chamber before June 8th, in order to prepare all procedures. This is extremely important, and a special announcement is made to this effect.

Discussion Today

Xunxin Shipyard Strike Hearing Yesterday 119

The Xunxin Shipyard strike has been going on for several days. Qiu Peihao of the Social Affairs Bureau was dispatched to mediate. Yesterday, he, along with representatives of the shipyard's union, went to the shipyard to negotiate. The shipyard consistently insisted on paying only one day's wages for the strike period, while the union believed that the employer was deliberately being evasive and was very angry. After the Social Affairs Bureau tried hard to mediate, the union representatives complied with the mediation and expressed their willingness to compromise, but insisted on a minimum of half wages for the strike period. However, the employer consistently insisted on one day's wages, resulting in a stalemate with no results. Since the shipyard strike, various unions, such as the shipping, woodworking, ink making, pharmaceutical, and postal unions, have gone to express their condolences and offered considerable assistance.

Presenting an Order from the Executive Yuan for the Municipal Government to Retract Its Mandate

All employees of the Commercial Press were very excited and demanded that the Reconstruction Committee of the Commercial Press Employees in Distress convene a congress to discuss countermeasures after learning that the Municipal Government had approved the dismissal conditions proposed by the employer. The committee presented a petition to the Executive Yuan of the National Government, ordering the Shanghai Municipal Government to retract its mandate (the petition is recorded below), and ordered all departments to convene member congresses. Yesterday (the 8th), the compilation department held a meeting at the Central Western Restaurant, attended by over a hundred members. Zhou Songjiu was elected as chairman and Zhu Tongzhou recorded the minutes. First, Zhu Gongchui and Chen Jiaxuan reported on the progress of negotiations, and Zhu Tongzhou reported on the economic situation of the meeting. Subsequently, the following resolutions were passed: (1) Continue the past spirit and fight to the end, vowing to achieve the goal of resuming work. (2) In addition to the original committee members, Zheng Xinnan and eight others were added as committee members. (3) The cost of the shelter will be borne by the Welfare Committee. Furthermore, the colleagues of the general affairs department of the library convened a member congress at the Sichuan Youth Association. Feng Yixian was chairman and Huang Deming was the recorder. First, Chen Dongwu, a standing committee member of the association, reported on the company's negotiations and the approval of the Social Affairs Bureau. The Welfare Committee was very willing to solicit the opinions of the members and sent a letter to the company, insisting on resuming work. Subsequently, Dong Yunting and Wang Shoukang reported on the shelter and the contact with lawyers Chen Qun and He Shizhen. It was unanimously advocated to persevere to the end and oppose dismissal. Later, Zhang Xinxiong and six others were added as directors. The printing department colleagues convened a meeting at the shelter, unanimously passing a resolution to insist on resuming work and petitioning the municipal government. It is reported that the colleagues of the distribution department also plan to convene a congress today to plan countermeasures together. The Commercial Press Employees' petition to the Executive Yuan is as follows: "Respectfully submit that the Commercial Press has deceived the authorities and dismissed employees, causing panic over unemployment and depriving workers of their interests. We appeal to order the Shanghai Municipal Government to retract its mandate in order to relieve the difficulties of workers and maintain the people's livelihood. The Commercial Press Shanghai Zhabei General Factory was destroyed by the violent Japanese army, and thousands of employees also suffered great disasters, living in poverty and displacement. For three months, Wang Yunwu, the director of the press, not only did not provide any relief after the incident, but also refused to return the compulsory savings that the employees had stored in the press. He intended to force the employees to accept and submit to harsh conditions through a scorched earth strategy. Recently, because the cunning plan failed, he again deceptively presented it to the Shanghai Municipal Government for approval of dismissal, placing thousands of employees who survived the disaster on the brink of despair. Such absurd measures are painful because the Shanghai Municipal Government disregards the true facts, legal agreements, and the suffering of the people, and is deceived by it. The press was founded with a capital of only a few thousand yuan. Through years of business expansion, shares have been added to shares, and the assets have now reached tens of millions. This incident was a national disaster, and there were some losses, but only half of the assets were lost. The government should find ways to maintain the press, but how can it exploit the sweat and blood of the employees who have made contributions to culture for decades to fill the gap? According to reason, how can this be considered fair? Moreover, the remaining property of the press is still more than double the amount. It is now actively engaged in restoration. The new Shanghai factory has been established, and the Beijing and Hong Kong branch factories have been greatly expanded. Dozens of branches are operating as usual. The proposed dismissal is even more unjustified. As for the regulations on retirement pay and severance pay, they are recorded in the company's treatment regulations and are observed by both labor and management. Now, under the situation of not being bankrupt, it wants to violate the law and reason, break the agreement, and take the opportunity to oppress, which is even more obvious. The Shanghai Municipal Government, based only on the one-sided words of the press, sacrifices the jobs of 4,000 employees, making them homeless, or even forcing them to take risks, which is not fortunate for the locality. The association is in this situation, not only feeling the great difficulties of the workers' lives in the future, but also worrying about social unrest, which will cause many hidden worries. Therefore, we appeal to your hospital to uphold justice, and to promptly order the Shanghai Municipal Government to retract its mandate for the press to deceive the authorities and dismiss employees without reason, in order to relieve the difficulties of workers and maintain the people's livelihood. We are sincerely waiting for orders. respectfully presented to the Executive Yuan of the National Government, Wang."
