Education Circles in Hubei Refuse the Director of the Education Department, Shen. They Also Demand Back Pay from the Provincial Government. Chairman Xia's Reply Is Satisfactory. Hankou Correspondence: The provincial schools and educational institutions in Hubei Province held a meeting at the Science Experiment Hall at 8:00 AM on the 6th to demand back pay and refuse the newly appointed Director of the Education Department, Shen Shiyuan. They decided to petition the provincial government. After the discussion, they marched in formation, led by Zhou Jingfang and Xia Zhizhong, to the provincial government. They submitted a petition to Chairman Xia. At the time, the provincial government was holding a routine meeting. The provincial committee members Kong Geng and Sun Sheng received them. Representatives from the education sector, including Chen Wenshan, stated their demands and submitted a letter refusing Shen, as well as demands regarding the arrears and equal treatment in future salary payments. Kong and Sun promised to convey their demands. The representatives remained standing until 1:00 PM when Chairman Xia Douyin finally found time to meet them. He replied to two points: (1) Director Shen was appointed by the central government. As subordinates, we must obey orders from above and cannot accommodate the representatives' request. However, it is also possible that Director Shen will not come due to your refusal. When the time comes to select a successor, we must determine a standard for suitability in order to request instructions from the central government. (2) The allocation of educational funds will be equal to all government agencies. The arrears will also be processed and distributed equally, without discrimination. The representatives deemed this satisfactory and left the provincial government, returning to the Science Experiment Hall to continue their discussions. Regarding the selection of a successor, they decided not to recommend anyone, but the person must meet the following conditions: (1) able to raise educational funds, (2) excellent in character and scholarship, (3) suitable for the position and the local situation, (4) impartial and selfless. They will submit a document to Chairman Xia to forward to the central government. The petition is as follows: "Submitting a petition regarding Shen Shiyuan, Director of the Hubei Education Department, who is deficient in knowledge, lacks experience, has a base character, and is unsuitable for the position. We earnestly request investigation and forwarding to the central government for swift dismissal and appointment of a capable person to maintain education. Hubei education has suffered repeated devastation and is on the verge of bankruptcy. Maintaining and saving it depends on a capable person. Recently, the provincial government was reorganized, and all aspects of governance were renewed. We hoped that education would be improved to meet the people's expectations. Unexpectedly, new appointments were made repeatedly (initially, Wang Shijie was appointed, but Wang declined; then Huang Jianzhong was appointed, but Huang also declined; finally, Shen Shiyuan was appointed). In fact, Shen Shiyuan, who is despised by the literati, was appointed to this important position. This is akin to replacing beams with inferior materials, causing great harm. We feel deeply concerned and dare not remain silent. Therefore, we have made repeated appeals and submitted numerous documents and telegrams. For the past ten days, we have been grateful for your consideration of the situation and your willingness to accommodate us. However, the central government does not understand the truth and has not changed its decision. We fear that the situation will not be communicated upwards and will cause future harm. We respectfully present the reasons for refusing Shen to you. Shen graduated from Waseda University in Japan, where he studied law, not education. He then served as the Director of General Affairs and part-time lecturer at Peking University. After the establishment of the National Government, he managed to obtain the position of Secretary-General of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, but was dismissed by Chairman Zhang for dereliction of duty within a few days. Currently, he is a secretary with simplified appointment at the Ministry of Education, but he has not actually reported for duty, only receiving a monthly salary and enjoying a leisurely life in Shanghai and Hangzhou. Therefore, he has no so-called knowledge or experience. Furthermore, Shen was a staff member at Peking University who repeatedly stirred up student movements, leading young students in factional and power struggles. The scar on his forehead remains to this day. Recently, in order to avoid reporting for duty, he has resorted to servile means to deceive Chairman Chiang and Minister Zhu, acting as a go-between in the hope of achieving his personal desires. Considering past events and observing recent situations, his base character is evident. We believe that Your Excellency, who respects your hometown and seeks to govern with diligence, should not allow such an unqualified person with no virtue or talent to fill the ranks. Moreover, Shen is in league with Huang Jianzhong, willingly acting as a puppet. How can we expect him to assist in provincial governance, improve education, and benefit our hometown? To prevent harm, action should be taken early. We respectfully implore Your Excellency, who has always been concerned about protecting education, to not allow this unqualified Shen Shiyuan to bring shame to the party and the country, and to poison the Jianghan region. Therefore, we dare to send representatives to meet with you and present our case in person. We earnestly request investigation and forwarding to the central government for swift dismissal of Shen Shiyuan from the position of Director of the Education Department, and the appointment of a capable person to maintain education. We are filled with anxiety and await your orders." (May 6) Zhejiang Province's Method for Subsidizing Education Expenses in Border Areas: Establishes Three Standards Based on Population and Region. Zhejiang Province believes that the people in the border counties are intellectually underdeveloped and have no understanding of the national situation or their own position. This situation is entirely due to the lack of popular education. Therefore, it has proposed a method for subsidizing education expenses in impoverished border areas, which will be implemented by the Finance and Education Departments after discussion. (1) The provincial government will make an overall plan to subsidize each county related to national defense with a certain amount of funding. (2) The subsidy standards will be divided into three categories based on population, area, and the level of educational development: Category 1: large population, large area, education expenses above 20,000 yuan; Category 2: large population, large area, education expenses above 30,000 yuan; Category 3: small population, small area, education expenses below 20,000 yuan. (3) The county administrative council will pass the plan and submit it to the provincial government for implementation. The Zhejiang Education Department Emphasizes Basic Education. Establishes Kindergarten Teacher Training School to Train Teachers. Counties and Cities Should Appropriately Establish Kindergartens. The Zhejiang Education Department believes that kindergarten education is the foundation of all education. If there is a lack of comprehensive facilities, it will have a significant impact on the future of education. It has been found that the Zhejiang Provincial Government has traditionally neglected kindergarten education. Few elementary schools in counties and cities have attached kindergartens. Even if they are established, there is a lack of qualified teachers. Therefore, it has been decided to establish a provincial kindergarten teacher training school in the 21st year to train kindergarten teachers, and to establish a model kindergarten and nursery to study the points that need to be improved in the existing kindergarten facilities, to regulate the standards for establishing kindergartens, and to urge the education bureaus of county and city governments to appropriately establish kindergartens and nurseries, in order to gradually promote this. Temporary Meeting of the Chinese Cooperative Society. Decides to Establish a Wholesale Agency Department. The Chinese Cooperative Society, recognizing the difficulties faced by cooperative societies in various regions, which are mostly due to the inconvenience of wholesale and the high prices charged by wholesalers, making it extremely difficult to develop business, and based on suggestions from the society to establish a wholesale agency department, which it also believes would greatly benefit cooperative societies in various regions, the executive committee members of the society, Chen Guofu, Zheng Shiying, and Chen Zhongming, drafted the articles of association. Chen Guofu chaired the meeting and Chen Zhongming recorded the minutes. After unanimous discussion, it was decided to revise and pass the proposed articles of association, and to send letters to cooperative societies in various regions to solicit opinions and actively prepare, in order to realize the establishment of the department as soon as possible. Commercial News: Fluctuations in the Gold Market Over the Past Week. Unpredictable Weather. Inevitable Minor Reaction After Nine Consecutive Weeks of Gains. Last week, the gold market experienced drastic fluctuations, rising and falling, ultimately proving unstoppable. Dealers were disoriented, with twists and turns of several to more than ten taels, making it extremely difficult to predict. This was due to conflicting domestic and international news, with market conditions shifting accordingly. It coincided with the spring race season for Western merchants, so trading was only half a day in the morning, as usual. The market trended upward from the beginning of the week, opening at 733.5 taels and then surging past 740 taels. On Wednesday, a new price of 747.2 yuan was seen, due to repeated reports of shrinkage in British silver, while American silver remained stable. This led to an upward trend in exchange rates, resulting in tight Shanghai taels and stable US dollars. Dealers' hedging was varied, with gold prices fluctuating irregularly, and both bulls and bears controlling each other. Towards the weekend, a sudden storm broke out, breaking through 30 taels and suddenly falling to 24.5 taels, due to the spread of various unfavorable news for the gold market, which changed the atmosphere for the worse. This was actually due to the influence of the Guangbang Hengxing bulls emerging. However, the exchange rate was able to stabilize, so the closing price was set, amounting to 80 taels, compared to 60 to 70 taels at the beginning of the week. Currently, some banks are absorbing spot gold, but inventory is not excessive. It has been found that the high and low prices in this week's gold market differed by 22.7 taels, with a net decrease of 2.1 yuan, which is due to a minor correction after nine consecutive weeks of gains. Here is a summary of the overall situation of the week. A Recap of the Entire Process. (Monday) (May 2) The big bar of silver shrunk by .0625, American silver remained unchanged, and there was no increase or decrease in the British-American exchange rate. However, the internal market tightened, due to the British-American Tobacco Company settling accounts, and the gold dealers also hedging. As for the June gold tender, it initially opened with an increase of 3.3 yuan, at 733.5 taels, as the private telegraphic silver price had shrunk by .125, and sentiment was good. It then retreated from 34.5 taels to 32.2 yuan, due to the likelihood of more sellers. Furthermore, the exchange rate was tight, and there were rumors of cash being issued, so it was 38 taels at noon. It then closed at 36.9 yuan, continuing the increase of 6.7 yuan from last Saturday, with a fluctuation of 5.8 yuan between the high and low. Trading was suspended in the afternoon due to the spring races. On this day, the exchange still accepted public orders (May spot). It is now being recovered by Run Chang, with an estimate of 3,700 bars, while more than ten firms have released them. (Tuesday) The big bar of silver shrunk again by .1875, silver price shrunk by .125, the opening price of Sterling remained the same, then revised to shrink by one grade, the domestic market was brisk, the dealers abandoned England and dumped the United States, but the gold tender initially fell by nine yuan, to 736 taels, because the price of silver shrunk and owed more, later only counted 32 taels, followed by a sudden rise, because there were rumors that more than 2,000 bars of spot goods were exported, plus a certain bank opened 400 bars, the buyers in the market are very constant, Dalian Gang and Guang Gang bought, the Sterling was further shrunk, so the market price went straight to the sky, even rushed out 40 taels, to 46 taels at noon, until closing at 45.1 yuan, up 8.2 yuan compared with the previous day, 14 taels review in half a day, also said to be huge. Bond Market for the Week After the Securities Exchange Resumed Operations: Prices Stable and Fluctuations Peaceful. Turnover Only Over 14 Million. Since the Japanese invasion of Shanghai and the suspension of operations of the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange, three months have passed in an instant. Although there have been repeated rumors of resumption of operations, they have ultimately not been realized due to military relations. It was not until the end of last month that the Ministry of Finance issued instructions, approving the opening of the market at the beginning of last week. Because the surrounding situation has improved and the Sino-Japanese issue in Shanghai has been resolved, the market is optimistic. Although large investors are still in a wait-and-see state, scattered investments are not deserted. Bond prices have generally trended upward. On Monday, except for the two types of consolidated six customs duties, all other types have risen to the limit and trading has been suspended. On Tuesday, there was a report of continued trading being suspended due to troop reduction. Although there were still increases, the fluctuations have been largely peaceful. However, since then, the market supply and demand situation has been flat, and although prices have fluctuated, the trend has gradually become sluggish, with no major changes in daily trading. However, it should be noted that the bond price increases and trading suspensions last week refer to the book prices on January 25. Compared to the off-market prices at the end of last month, the fluctuations are very small. Compared to January, the actual increase is very large, excluding accrued principal and interest. Internal troop reduction has almost increased by 10 yuan, and other good types have increased by about 5 or 6 yuan. Judging from the current situation of the bond market, unless there are new changes in the surrounding situation, there will not be major increases or decreases in the short term, and the future may be sluggish. In terms of bond market trading, spot transactions are not deserted. Total turnover for the week reached 574,200 yuan, including 99,500 yuan for 19 Customs, 89,000 yuan each for salt tax, unified tax, and 20 Customs, and 670,000 yuan each for troop retrenchment and 20 Customs. Other types were only around 1 million yuan. Although 96 and financial products were issued, the amount was very small. There were also not many transactions for June futures. Cotton yarn prices continued to trend downward last week, due to unstable conditions, inconvenient transportation, and tight finances. In addition, last year's severe floods caused significant damage to all parties, and now the Shanghai war has broken out again, tightening the money supply. The economic situation in the interior is particularly difficult, with a significant lack of purchasing power. As a result, business is extremely sluggish, leading to a gradual increase in factory inventories. The goods of the Wuxi Yarn Factory have been transported to Shanghai in order to find a way out. The yarn from the Zhengzhou Yarn Factory is also being sold in Shanghai, which shows the difficulty of selling yarn in all directions. As a result, prices have continued to decline. The standard yarn for yarn and cloth trading officially resumed on Monday, with the standard changed to 20s "Ren Zhong," which is one grade higher than before, but the price was very low, only 155.3 taels. It coincided with a major slump in American cotton, and rumors of war were rampant. Those outside the industry viewed the surrounding environment as harsh and unanimously tended to sell off. The market gradually declined. The lowest price on Thursday was 150 taels. At the weekend, due to the official signing of the Sino-Japanese Peace Ceasefire Agreement, sentiment was shaken, and the situation rebounded strongly. The total transaction volume of standard yarn for the week was 53,000 bales. The current yarn purchased by various groups was estimated at 4,371 bales. The prices of 32s and 42s fell by 6-7 taels, and the prices of 16s and 20s fell by 2-3 taels. Shenxin sometimes opened for business. Yesterday's News on the Workers' Strike at the "Shishi Xinbao" 122

Since the "Shishi Xinbao" newspaper in Shanghai dismissed all of its workers under the pretext of the "Da Wanbao" newspaper printing incident, a labor-capital dispute has arisen. The situation has been reported in various newspapers. For over a month, despite mediators' efforts, the matter remains unresolved due to the newspaper's lack of sincerity. The union, fearing that the public is not fully aware of the case, has issued a statement to clarify where the responsibility lies. The workers forced to leave the newspaper have also started fundraising. Here are the reports from yesterday:

Forced Workers Start Fundraising: After being dismissed by the management, all workers of the newspaper, while waiting for the union to actively negotiate with the management, have organized a publicity and fundraising team to fight to the end. It is reported that in recent days, they have already raised 100 yuan from Mr. Sun Ke, 20 yuan from Ms. He Xiangning, and 20 yuan from Mr. Ma Chaojun. These gentlemen have also expressed their deep sympathy and offered words of comfort.

Statement by Spokesperson of the Newspaper Industry Union: It has been over a month since the labor dispute at the newspaper began. The losses suffered by both labor and management are substantial. Upon detailed analysis, the responsibility for this loss should be borne by the newspaper. As the Japanese invaders encroach and the national crisis intensifies, all those with breath and spirit are filled with grief and anger, united against the enemy. How could we, the labor force, rise up and make demands from domestic capital during this time of crisis? The labor force, whose vision and knowledge are typically considered immature, has such insight during this time of national crisis. Yet the capital, whose vision and knowledge far surpass that of the labor force, especially the capital of newspapers staffed by intellectuals, should have even greater patriotic vision during this national crisis, setting an example for the masses and fulfilling the duty of our press. The "Shishi Xinbao" management, during this national crisis, unreasonably refused to allow workers who have served the newspaper for many years and made no prior demands to work. One wonders what their intentions are. The workers who were refused work are in a situation where, on one hand, their homes in the war zone have been destroyed, leaving them with nowhere to settle. On the other hand, they are being forced into unemployment, leaving their future livelihood without guarantee. Unable to bear it, they have started fundraising from all sectors of society and detailing the various vicious tactics of the newspaper's management, so that the public can understand the truth. This kind of work can be described as the arduous and remarkable work of our newspaper workers. The "Shishi Xinbao" usually uses editorials to advocate for relieving unemployment and guiding society. Furthermore, when the tensions of the Battle of Shanghai were high, they did not hesitate to sacrifice newspaper space to publish job advertisements for free to help those displaced by the war. On the surface, the public praised them for this. One would think that with such a compassionate newspaper, the Chinese nation would not perish. Little did people know that the newspaper's management was taking advantage of the national crisis to hire unemployed workers at low prices and reduce the workload of its existing employees to achieve the goal of suppressing workers and undermining the union. Our newspaper workers have finally realized the true nature of the newspaper's management's actions: their so-called relief for unemployment and leadership of society are nothing more than hypocritical and despicable tactics to deceive themselves and others. As for the cause of this labor dispute, the facts are very clear and need no further elaboration. Therefore, the responsibility for the loss should be borne by the management.

Tsinghua Alumni Association Dinner 123

The Shanghai Tsinghua Alumni Association, due to the impact of the suspension of the Boxer Indemnity funds for one year on Tsinghua University President Mei Yuehan and the Secretary of the China Education and Culture Foundation, Ren Hongjun, who came south to discuss the matter, the president of the Alumni Association, Cai Jingping, has scheduled a meeting on Tuesday, the 10th of this month, at 6:00 PM at the Bank Club to welcome them. They have also invited Sichuan entrepreneur Lu Zuofu to speak about his decade-plus of hard work and perseverance in running various industries in Sichuan. It is expected to be a grand occasion.

Hu Zhenbiao Illegally Recruits Soldiers 124

Yu Yongyuan, a sixteen-year-old boy from Jinhua, came to Shanghai from Hangzhou with his mother a few days ago. Unexpectedly, he lost his way and became separated from his mother, leaving him with nowhere to go. As he wandered the streets, Hu Zhenbiao, a twenty-two-year-old man from Zhenjiang who lives in a small hotel in the French Concession, saw that Yu Yongyuan was young and easily deceived. He invited Yu to join the army, but Yu refused. Hu Zhenbiao insisted on taking Yu Yongyuan to Zhenjiang. Yesterday at 2:00 PM, they quarreled and fought on Xinqiao Street. A police officer, Yang Zhengtu, saw them and, considering Hu's private recruitment of soldiers a violation of the ban, took them both to the First Precinct of the Second District for questioning. After Director Xu interrogated them and confirmed the details, a military certificate from the 9th Division of the Army and a badge of a transport officer, Ma Zhigui, were found on Hu. Neither belonged to Hu, clearly indicating illegal recruitment. He was sentenced to be handed over to the General Bureau for legal action.

A Prodigal Son Commits Suicide by Drowning 125

An old woman, Zhang Chen, is sixty-eight years old and has only one son, Zhang Ren, who is twenty-seven years old. He used to be a carpenter, is married, and has two sons, one of whom has already died, and the other is four years old. Zhang Ren was spoiled by his parents from a young age, leading to a lazy nature. He has been unemployed for several years and is deeply addicted to opium, which is destroying the family fortune. Since his father's death, he has sold off most of the family property, and the family is without food. As a result, his wife relies on her parents' family for food, and his old mother works as a helper for the wealthy to make a living. Only Zhang Ren is alone and unrepentant, wandering aimlessly and indulging in opium dens. Thus, in this chilling weather, he wears only thin, short clothes and has exhausted all his resources. Instead of embracing a positive outlook, he has turned to a negative path and committed suicide by drowning the day before yesterday. Yesterday, his body floated to the shore. The seventh district local security officer recovered the body and identified it. Zhang Chen went to identify the body and confirmed that it was her son. She immediately petitioned the local court for an exemption from autopsy and requested a free coffin because she could not afford one. After preliminary examination by Prosecutor Xie, the request for exemption from autopsy was granted, and a note was issued to the Charity Hall to request a coffin for burial.

Genuine American Saigon Cinnamon Arrives in Shanghai 126

Most of the Saigon cinnamon used in Chinese medicine is not produced domestically and relies on imports from North and South America. However, it is mostly transshipped from Japan to China for sale, with the Japanese reaping the profits. The total value of imports through Japan each year is no less than several hundred thousand yuan. Now, the Chinese merchant Hanli Company (located at No. 467 Jiangxi Road, opposite the Water Pavilion) has recognized this situation and directly purchases and transports it from overseas, reselling it to medicine merchants in various regions to meet demand. This is truly an important undertaking in the movement to resist foreign goods. Moreover, the quality of the goods is pure, and the prices are fair, which is especially commendable.

New Houses for Rent in Shunanli 127

The Shunj Company has recently built dozens of three-story buildings in Xixiangs Road, French Concession. The style is new and the light is plentiful. It is the safest area in Shanghai. Take the No. 21 bus from the foreign Hongqiao. Get off at Guangci Hospital. The transportation is very convenient. The rent is low and there is no small rent charged. There are few houses left. Those who want to rent can contact the accounting office in the neighborhood.

Minutes of the Shanghai Dock Workers' Consolidation Association Meeting 132

The Shanghai Dock Workers' Consolidation Association held its 30th Consolidation Committee meeting yesterday. Chairman Shen Wenyuan performed the formalities, and after reporting, the following was discussed: (1) The date of the Association's regular meeting. It was decided that it would be held every Wednesday and Saturday at 3:00 PM. (2) The case of arrears of salary to the members and staff of the Association. It was decided that from May 1st, each member and staff member would serve in a purely voluntary capacity. All previous arrears of old salary would be repaid in succession after the outstanding fees from each dock were collected to complete the formalities. (3) The case of the monthly fee for the Blue Funnel Wharf. It was decided to inform the wharf that all monthly fees from April of this year would be paid as usual.

It is learned that the school will hold lectures and public exhibitions every Sunday, and will hold a grand exhibition at the Central Stadium on June 4th. Preparations are currently underway.

Lili Company's Car Stolen 135

By Chauffeur Qiu Buyun

The Lili Automobile Company at No. 225 Tongfu Road, West Shanghai, suddenly had a car stolen by someone who drove it away without permission a few days ago. The car is worth 2,300 taels of silver. After repeated investigations by the company's manager, Li Songquan, it was learned that it was stolen by the chauffeur, Qiu Buyun, in between times. He immediately reported to the Jing'an Temple Patrol Room, which sent Detective Huang Yongquan to arrest the chauffeur yesterday. He will be sent to the First Special District Local Court for questioning.

Yong'an Cotton Mill Robbery Suspect Arrested 136

At around 9:00 AM yesterday, Western Detective Dong Aiqi and Chinese Detective Liu Chunshu from the Public Concession Gordon Road Patrol Room, along with the criminal Ma Dongsheng, reported to the Sixth District Police Station in Caojiadu, West Shanghai, that Zhang Huizhang and others, wanted criminals in the case of a gang robbery at the Yong'an Cotton Mill on April 15th, were hiding at No. 11 Xingyuli, Bailinan Road. They requested that police be sent to assist in the arrest. The district chief sent police officers along with the detectives to the address and arrested the criminal Zhang Huizhang. After a brief interrogation in the district, he was handed over to the detectives to be taken back to the patrol room for further investigation.

Weather Report 137

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the sky along the coast of Shandong was mostly cloudy with gentle northerly winds. The sky in this area along the coast and in the Yangtze River basin was overcast, with heavy fog in the morning. The wind was unstable. The coast south of Ma'an Island was cloudy with fog, and there were areas with no wind. There was a cyclone and rain in southern Japan, due to a low pressure system passing through and moving east or northeast. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the local temperature was 61.3 degrees at its highest and 52.7 degrees at its lowest. On the same day last year, the highest was 71.2 degrees and the lowest was 47.1 degrees.
